    I-p2-015 (#754): plan-review page = run-start surface (unblocks #761 dashboard-monitoring)
    
    New /plan page relocates run-start off the dashboard. 'Confirm + start': question
    display-only (edit → /intake); re-runs the FULL intake gate (runIntake clinical+PICO,
    not the lenient /scope/check) on mount so direct-nav is gated identically; Start
    enabled ONLY for in_scope + disambiguation-resolved (mandatory ambiguity preflight
    #505 preserved). Honest 'what POLARIS will do' plan (ties to corpus-approval gate).
    Question-only (no uploads → immutable question → one-time check valid; uploads keep
    /upload home until a follow-up). createRun → /runs/[id]; ConcurrentRunError handled.
    Intake gains 'Continue to plan →' on in_scope (same PR, no dead-end). Codex brief
    APPROVE iter2; typecheck + build green; screenshot-verified.
    
    Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.7 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>

diff --git a/web/app/plan/page.tsx b/web/app/plan/page.tsx
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..d3174602
--- /dev/null
+++ b/web/app/plan/page.tsx
@@ -0,0 +1,356 @@
+// I-p2-015 (#754): Plan review — the run-start surface (relocated off the
+// dashboard so #761 can become monitoring-only). "Confirm + start": the
+// question is DISPLAY-ONLY here (single source of preflight truth = intake);
+// editing routes back to /intake. On mount it re-runs the FULL intake gate
+// (runIntake — the clinical + PICO classifier, NOT the lenient /scope/check) so
+// direct navigation to /plan?q=… is gated identically. "Start research run" is
+// enabled ONLY for an in_scope, disambiguation-resolved question. Question-only
+// run-start (no uploads here — document grounding keeps its /upload home until a
+// follow-up wires it into this flow).
+"use client";
+
+import {
+  ArrowLeft,
+  BadgeCheck,
+  FileSearch,
+  Layers,
+  ShieldCheck,
+} from "lucide-react";
+import Link from "next/link";
+import { useRouter, useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
+import { Suspense, useEffect, useState } from "react";
+
+import { DisambiguationModal } from "@/app/intake/components/disambiguation_modal";
+import { ErrorState } from "@/components/states/state_kit";
+import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
+import {
+  ConcurrentRunError,
+  createRun,
+  runDisambiguation,
+  runIntake,
+  type DisambiguationCluster,
+  type IntakeScopeDecision,
+  type TemplateId,
+} from "@/lib/api";
+
+const TEMPLATE_IDS: readonly TemplateId[] = [
+  "clinical",
+  "policy",
+  "tech",
+  "ai_sovereignty",
+  "canada_us",
+  "due_diligence",
+  "custom",
+  "workforce",
+];
+
+function asTemplate(value: string | null): TemplateId {
+  return value && (TEMPLATE_IDS as readonly string[]).includes(value)
+    ? (value as TemplateId)
+    : "clinical";
+}
+
+const PLAN_STEPS = [
+  {
+    icon: FileSearch,
+    title: "Retrieve primary sources",
+    body: "POLARIS searches via logged Canadian egress and snapshots each source it draws from.",
+  },
+  {
+    icon: ShieldCheck,
+    title: "Corpus-adequacy + approval gate",
+    body: "The source set must meet per-tier adequacy and pass the approval gate before any brief is generated.",
+  },
+  {
+    icon: Layers,
+    title: "Generate, then verify every claim",
+    body: "Each sentence is generated section by section, then span-verified against its primary source by an independent evaluator family.",
+  },
+  {
+    icon: BadgeCheck,
+    title: "Produce an auditable bundle",
+    body: "You get a brief where every claim links to the exact source passage behind it.",
+  },
+] as const;
+
+type State =
+  | { kind: "loading" }
+  | { kind: "ready"; decision: IntakeScopeDecision }
+  | { kind: "error"; message: string };
+
+function PlanContent() {
+  const router = useRouter();
+  const searchParams = useSearchParams();
+  const question = (searchParams.get("q") ?? "").trim();
+  const template = asTemplate(searchParams.get("template"));
+
+  const [state, setState] = useState<State>({ kind: "loading" });
+  const [disambigClusters, setDisambigClusters] = useState<
+    DisambiguationCluster[]
+  >([]);
+  const [disambigOpen, setDisambigOpen] = useState(false);
+  const [disambigResolved, setDisambigResolved] = useState(false);
+  const [starting, setStarting] = useState(false);
+  const [startError, setStartError] = useState<string | null>(null);
+  const [concurrent, setConcurrent] = useState<{
+    runId: string;
+    message: string;
+  } | null>(null);
+
+  // On mount: re-run the FULL intake gate over the (immutable) question. This
+  // is the same clinical + PICO classifier intake uses, so /plan is safe even
+  // when reached by direct URL.
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!question) {
+      setState({ kind: "error", message: "no-question" });
+      return;
+    }
+    let cancelled = false;
+    (async () => {
+      try {
+        const result = await runIntake(question);
+        if (cancelled) return;
+        setState({ kind: "ready", decision: result.decision });
+        if (
+          result.decision.needs_disambiguation &&
+          result.decision.candidate_snippets &&
+          result.decision.candidate_snippets.length > 0
+        ) {
+          const dis = await runDisambiguation(
+            result.decision.candidate_snippets,
+          );
+          if (cancelled) return;
+          if (dis.is_ambiguous && dis.clusters.length > 1) {
+            setDisambigClusters(dis.clusters);
+            setDisambigOpen(true);
+          } else {
+            setDisambigResolved(true); // nothing to disambiguate
+          }
+        } else {
+          setDisambigResolved(true);
+        }
+      } catch (err) {
+        if (cancelled) return;
+        setState({
+          kind: "error",
+          message:
+            err instanceof Error
+              ? err.message
+              : "Could not check this question.",
+        });
+      }
+    })();
+    return () => {
+      cancelled = true;
+    };
+  }, [question]);
+
+  if (
+    !question ||
+    (state.kind === "error" && state.message === "no-question")
+  ) {
+    return (
+      <section
+        data-testid="plan-page"
+        className="mx-auto flex w-full max-w-2xl flex-col gap-4 px-6 py-16 text-center"
+      >
+        <h1 className="text-foreground text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight">
+          Nothing to plan yet
+        </h1>
+        <p className="text-muted-foreground text-sm">
+          Start from a research question and POLARIS will lay out the plan
+          before running it.
+        </p>
+        <div>
+          <Button
+            nativeButton={false}
+            render={<Link href="/intake">Ask a question</Link>}
+          />
+        </div>
+      </section>
+    );
+  }
+
+  const decision = state.kind === "ready" ? state.decision : null;
+  const inScope = decision?.status === "in_scope";
+  const canStart = inScope && disambigResolved && !starting;
+
+  async function onStart() {
+    setStartError(null);
+    setConcurrent(null);
+    setStarting(true);
+    try {
+      const run = await createRun({ template, question, document_ids: [] });
+      router.push(`/runs/${run.run_id}`);
+    } catch (err) {
+      if (err instanceof ConcurrentRunError) {
+        setConcurrent({ runId: err.activeRunId, message: err.message });
+        setStarting(false);
+        return;
+      }
+      setStartError(
+        err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Could not start the run.",
+      );
+      setStarting(false);
+    }
+  }
+
+  function notInScopeMessage(d: IntakeScopeDecision): string {
+    switch (d.status) {
+      case "out_of_scope":
+        return "This question is outside POLARIS's clinical research scope.";
+      case "refused":
+        return "POLARIS declined this question (refusal-bait or unsafe request).";
+      case "ambiguous_needs_clarification":
+        return "This question needs clarification before it can be researched.";
+      default:
+        return "This question can't be started as written.";
+    }
+  }
+
+  return (
+    <section

+        <Link

+          className="text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground inline-flex w-fit items-center gap-1 text-xs"

+          Edit question
+        </Link>
+        <h1 className="text-foreground text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight sm:text-3xl">
+          Review the plan
+        </h1>
+        <p className="text-muted-foreground text-sm">
+          Confirm what POLARIS will research before the run starts.
+        </p>
+      </div>

+        <p className="text-foreground text-lg leading-relaxed font-medium">
+          {question}
+        </p>

+          <span className="border-border rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5">
+            Template: <span className="text-foreground">{template}</span>
+          </span>
+          {state.kind === "loading" ? (
+            <span>Checking scope…</span>
+          ) : decision?.scope_class ? (
+            <span className="border-border rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5">
+              Scope:{" "}
+              <span className="text-foreground">{decision.scope_class}</span>
+            </span>
+          ) : null}
+        </div>
+      </div>
+
+      {/* What POLARIS will do */}
+      <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
+        <h2 className="text-foreground text-sm font-semibold">
+          What POLARIS will do
+        </h2>
+        <ol className="grid gap-4 sm:grid-cols-2">
+          {PLAN_STEPS.map((step, i) => (
+            <li
+              key={step.title}
+              className="border-border bg-card flex flex-col gap-1.5 rounded-lg border p-4"
+            >
+              <div className="text-primary flex items-center gap-2">
+                <step.icon aria-hidden className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0" />
+                <span className="text-foreground text-sm font-medium">
+                  {i + 1}. {step.title}
+                </span>
+              </div>
+              <p className="text-muted-foreground text-xs leading-relaxed">
+                {step.body}
+              </p>
+            </li>
+          ))}
+        </ol>
+      </div>
+
+      {/* Not-in-scope guard */}
+      {decision && !inScope ? (
+        <div
+          role="alert"
+          data-testid="plan-blocked"
+          className="border-refusal/30 bg-refusal/10 flex flex-col gap-1 rounded-lg border p-4"
+        >
+          <p className="text-foreground text-sm font-medium">
+            Can't start this run
+          </p>
+          <p className="text-muted-foreground text-xs">
+            {notInScopeMessage(decision)} Edit the question to continue.
+          </p>
+        </div>
+      ) : null}
+
+      {startError ? (
+        <ErrorState title="Couldn't start the run" message={startError} />
+      ) : null}
+
+      {concurrent ? (
+        <div
+          role="alert"
+          data-testid="plan-concurrent"
+          className="border-contradiction/30 bg-contradiction/10 flex flex-col gap-1 rounded-lg border p-4"
+        >
+          <p className="text-foreground text-sm font-medium">
+            A run is already in progress
+          </p>
+          <p className="text-muted-foreground text-xs">{concurrent.message}</p>
+          <Link
+            href={`/runs/${concurrent.runId}`}
+            className="text-primary text-xs underline-offset-2 hover:underline"
+          >
+            View the active run →
+          </Link>
+        </div>
+      ) : null}
+
+      {/* Start */}
+      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
+        <Button
+          type="button"
+          data-testid="plan-start-run"
+          className="h-11 px-7"
+          disabled={!canStart}
+          onClick={onStart}
+        >
+          {starting ? "Starting…" : "Start research run"}
+        </Button>
+        <Button
+          variant="ghost"
+          nativeButton={false}
+          render={<Link href="/intake">Cancel</Link>}
+        />
+      </div>
+
+      <DisambiguationModal
+        open={disambigOpen}
+        clusters={disambigClusters}
+        onSelectCluster={() => {
+          setDisambigResolved(true);
+          setDisambigOpen(false);
+        }}
+        onCancel={() => setDisambigOpen(false)}
+      />
+    </section>
+  );
+}

+  return (
+    <Suspense fallback={null}>
+      <PlanContent />
+    </Suspense>
+  );

 193:           ) : null}
 194:         </>
 195:       ) : null}

 197:       <AmbiguityModal
 198:         open={modalOpen}
 199:         decision={state.kind === "ok" ? state.decision : null}
 200:         onContinue={() => setModalOpen(false)}
 201:         onCancel={() => setModalOpen(false)}
 202:       />

 205:         open={disambigOpen}
 206:         clusters={disambigClusters}
 207:         onSelectCluster={(cid) => {
 208:           const found = disambigClusters.find((c) => c.cluster_id === cid);
 209:           setPickedClusterLabel(found?.label ?? null);
 210:           setDisambigOpen(false);
 211:         }}
 212:         onCancel={() => setDisambigOpen(false)}
 213:       />
 214: 
 215:       <output data-testid="disambig-picked-label" className="sr-only">
 216:         {pickedClusterLabel ?? ""}
 217:       </output>

  81: function PlanContent() {

 101:   // is the same clinical + PICO classifier intake uses, so /plan is safe even

 103:   useEffect(() => {
 104:     if (!question) {
 105:       setState({ kind: "error", message: "no-question" });
 106:       return;
 107:     }
 108:     let cancelled = false;
 109:     (async () => {
 110:       try {
 111:         const result = await runIntake(question);
 112:         if (cancelled) return;
 113:         setState({ kind: "ready", decision: result.decision });
 114:         if (
 115:           result.decision.needs_disambiguation &&

 120:             result.decision.candidate_snippets,

 124:             setDisambigClusters(dis.clusters);

 126:           } else {
 127:             setDisambigResolved(true); // nothing to disambiguate
 128:           }
 129:         } else {
 130:           setDisambigResolved(true);
 131:         }
 132:       } catch (err) {

 136:           message:

 140:         });
 141:       }
 142:     })();

 144:       cancelled = true;
 145:     };
 146:   }, [question]);

 169:         </div>
 170:       </section>

 172:   }

 178:   async function onStart() {

 195:     }

 605: export async function runDisambiguation(
 606:   candidates: { text: string; embedding: number[] }[],
 607: ): Promise<DisambiguationResponse> {
 608:   const response = await authFetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/disambiguation`, {
 609:     method: "POST",

 622: export interface IntakeErrorBody {
 623:   error: true;
 624:   code: "too_short" | "too_long" | "invalid_input";
 625:   message: string;
 626:   raw: string;
 627: }
 628: 
 629: export class IntakeBadRequestError extends Error {
 630:   code: IntakeErrorBody["code"];
 631:   raw: string;
 632:   constructor(body: IntakeErrorBody) {
 633:     super(body.message);
 634:     this.name = "IntakeBadRequestError";
 635:     this.code = body.code;
 636:     this.raw = body.raw;
 637:   }
 638: }
 639: 
 640: export async function runIntake(
 641:   question: string,
 642: ): Promise<IntakeSuccessResponse> {
 643:   const response = await authFetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/intake`, {
 644:     method: "POST",
 645:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 646:     body: JSON.stringify({ question }),
 647:   });
 648: 
 649:   if (response.status === 400) {
 650:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 651:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as IntakeErrorBody | null;
 652:     if (body && body.error) {
 653:       throw new IntakeBadRequestError(body);
 654:     }
 655:   }
 656: 
 657:   return asJsonOrThrow<IntakeSuccessResponse>(response);
 658: }

   4:  * Mirrors the FastAPI contract in src/polaris_v6/api/{runs,health,stream}.py.
   5:  *
   6:  * I-carney-005 (2026-05-13): all requests are browser-relative paths so the
   7:  * browser only ever talks to the webui origin. Next.js server-side rewrites
   8:  * (web/next.config.ts) forward `/api/v6/*` → `${INTERNAL_API_URL}/*`, which
   9:  * in production compose is `http://api:8000` (a Docker service name the
  10:  * browser cannot resolve directly). In local dev, INTERNAL_API_URL defaults
  11:  * to http://localhost:8000 so `npm run dev` against a host-port-mapped
  12:  * backend works without any client-side configuration.
  13:  *
  14:  * Codex diff iter-1 P1-B: NEXT_PUBLIC_BACKEND_URL is no longer consulted at
  15:  * runtime — baking an absolute http://api:8000 into the client bundle would
  16:  * make production browsers attempt direct Docker-network reach and fail.
  17:  */
  18: 
  19: import { authHeader, redirectToSignIn } from "@/lib/auth";
  20: 
  21: const BACKEND_URL = "/api/v6";
  22: 
  23: /**
  24:  * I-rdy-004 (#500) — fetch wrapper for every v6 API call. Injects the
  25:  * `Authorization: Bearer <jwt>` header, preserves any caller-supplied
  26:  * headers, and does NOT force a content-type (so `FormData` uploads keep
  27:  * their auto-generated multipart boundary). On a 401 it clears the token
  28:  * and routes to /sign-in.
  29:  */
  30: async function authFetch(
  31:   url: string,
  32:   init: RequestInit = {},
  33: ): Promise<Response> {
  34:   const headers = new Headers(init.headers ?? {});
  35:   for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(authHeader())) {
  36:     headers.set(key, value);
  37:   }
  38:   const response = await globalThis.fetch(url, { ...init, headers });
  39:   if (response.status === 401) {
  40:     redirectToSignIn();
  41:   }
  42:   return response;
  43: }
  44: 
  45: /**
  46:  * I-rdy-004 — SSE URL for a run's event stream. Native `EventSource` cannot
  47:  * set request headers, so the JWT rides as the `access_token` query param;
  48:  * the backend `require_auth` accepts it for `/stream/*` paths only.
  49:  */
  50: export function streamUrl(runId: string): string {
  51:   const token = authHeader().Authorization?.replace(/^Bearer /, "");
  52:   const base = `${BACKEND_URL}/stream/${encodeURIComponent(runId)}`;
  53:   return token ? `${base}?access_token=${encodeURIComponent(token)}` : base;
  54: }

  72:   | "abort_scope_rejected"

  81: }

  83: export interface RunStatusResponse {
  84:   run_id: string;
  85:   status: RunStatus;
  86:   // I-ui-bug-001 (#725): the pipeline-A verdict (success / abort_* / partial_*
  87:   // / error_*), distinct from the lifecycle `status`. mark_aborted() stores
  88:   // lifecycle_status='completed' for aborts, so lifecycle alone CANNOT tell a
  89:   // successful run from an aborted one — pipeline_status is required to render
  90:   // a completed run honestly (an aborted run must NOT show as success).
  91:   pipeline_status?: string | null;
  92:   // I-rdy-011 (#507): true once a cancel has been requested; lets the run
  93:   // page show a cancel as in-flight before an in-progress run transitions.
  94:   cancel_requested?: boolean;
  95:   template: string;
  96:   question: string;
  97:   queued_at: string;
  98:   started_at?: string | null;
  99:   finished_at?: string | null;
 100: }
 101: 
 102: export interface ApiError extends Error {
 103:   status: number;
 104:   body: unknown;
 105: }
 106: 
 107: async function asJsonOrThrow<T>(response: Response): Promise<T> {
 108:   const body = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 109:   if (!response.ok) {
 110:     const error = new Error(
 111:       `POLARIS backend returned ${response.status}`,
 112:     ) as ApiError;
 113:     error.status = response.status;
 114:     error.body = body;
 115:     throw error;
 116:   }
 117:   return body as T;
 118: }
 119: 
 120: /**
 121:  * Thrown by createRun when POST /runs is rejected by the 1-concurrent-session
 122:  * constraint (I-rdy-013): a research run is already queued or in progress.
 123:  */
 124: export class ConcurrentRunError extends Error {
 125:   readonly activeRunId: string;
 126:   readonly activeStatus: string;
 127:   constructor(message: string, activeRunId: string, activeStatus: string) {
 128:     super(message);
 129:     this.name = "ConcurrentRunError";
 130:     this.activeRunId = activeRunId;
 131:     this.activeStatus = activeStatus;
 132:   }
 133: }
 134: 
 135: export async function createRun(
 136:   payload: RunRequest,
 137: ): Promise<RunStatusResponse> {
 138:   const response = await authFetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/runs`, {
 139:     method: "POST",
 140:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 141:     body: JSON.stringify(payload),
 142:   });
 143:   if (response.status === 409) {
 144:     // Read the body exactly once, then unwrap FastAPI's { detail: {...} }
 145:     // envelope. The 1-concurrent-session reject carries a structured detail;
 146:     // any other 409 falls through to a generic ApiError.
 147:     const body = (await response.json().catch(() => null)) as {
 148:       detail?: unknown;
 149:     } | null;
 150:     const detail = (body?.detail ?? body) as {
 151:       code?: string;
 152:       message?: string;
 153:       active_run_id?: string;
 154:       active_status?: string;
 155:     } | null;
 156:     if (detail && detail.code === "concurrent_run_active") {
 157:       throw new ConcurrentRunError(
 158:         detail.message ?? "A research run is already in progress.",
 159:         detail.active_run_id ?? "",
 160:         detail.active_status ?? "in_progress",
 161:       );
 162:     }
 163:     const error = new Error("POLARIS backend returned 409") as ApiError;
 164:     error.status = 409;
 165:     error.body = body;
 166:     throw error;
 167:   }
 168:   return asJsonOrThrow<RunStatusResponse>(response);
 169: }
 170: 
 171: export async function getRun(runId: string): Promise<RunStatusResponse> {
 172:   const response = await authFetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/runs/${runId}`);
 173:   return asJsonOrThrow<RunStatusResponse>(response);
 174: }

 180:   const response = await authFetch(

docs\transparency.md:70:What Serper receives: the search query string itself, plus the normal request metadata any HTTP API call carries — the API account/key, source IP, timestamp, and user-agent — which Serper's privacy policy (serper.dev/privacy) describes it logging as system/access activity. What Serper does NOT receive: the uploaded corpus, the evidence pool, the generated report, or any operator-entered content. Serper returns only result URLs + snippets; POLARIS then fetches the actual T1 evidence directly from the government corpus endpoints listed above.
docs\transparency.md:78:**Tier-1 evidence fetching under lockdown.** Pipeline-A's sovereignty filter accepts only T1 (regulatory + clinical guideline) sources by default. Arbitrary publisher domains (nature.com, nejm.org, thelancet.com, etc.) are NOT in the allowlist — they're T2/T3 and excluded by the sovereignty filter anyway; the egress drop is defense-in-depth.

 succeeded in 1487ms:
   1: """Runs router — POST /runs, GET /runs/{id}, POST /runs/{id}/cancel.
   2: 
   3: I-phase0-005 (Codex APPROVE iter 4): persist runs to SQLite via
   4: polaris_v6.queue.run_store and enqueue the Dramatiq actor on POST.
   5: Replaces the previous in-memory `_run_table` dict.
   6: 
   7: I-rdy-010 (#506): POST /runs resolves uploaded `document_ids` to content
   8: BEFORE inserting/enqueuing the run, so a missing or unparsed upload fails
   9: loud here rather than leaving a queued orphan run. The resolved content is
  10: embedded in the actor message because the Dramatiq worker is a separate
  11: process and cannot read the API process's in-memory upload table.
  12: 
  13: I-rdy-011 (#507): POST /runs/{id}/cancel — a queued run cancels instantly;
  14: an in-progress run records the cancel request (the worker observes it at
  15: the next pipeline stage boundary). Already-terminal runs are an idempotent
  16: no-op.
  17: 
  18: I-rdy-013 (#509): POST /runs enforces the 1-concurrent-session constraint
  19: via `run_store.insert_run_if_idle` — a 2nd concurrent request is cleanly
  20: rejected with HTTP 409 (never enqueued) and a structured detail the
  21: frontend renders as a link to the active run.
  22: """
  23: 
  24: from __future__ import annotations
  25: 
  26: import sqlite3
  27: import uuid
  28: 
  29: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
  30: 
  31: from polaris_v6.api.upload import chunk_text, get_upload_record
  32: from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
  33: from polaris_v6.queue.actors import enqueue_research_run
  34: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_request import RunRequest
  35: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  36: 
  37: router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["runs"])
  38: 
  39: 
  40: def _resolve_uploaded_documents(document_ids: list[str]) -> list[dict]:
  41:     """Resolve uploaded document_ids → content for actor-message embedding.
  42: 
  43:     Returns one dict per id: `{document_id, classification, filename,
  44:     chunks}`. `chunks` is `chunk_text(record.content)` — the full document
  45:     re-chunked (and capped), NOT the 3-chunk `chunk_preview`.
  46: 
  47:     Fails loud (HTTP 400) per LAW II on:
  48:       * a document_id with no upload record;
  49:       * an upload that yields no extractable text (e.g. an unparsed
  50:         pdf/docx) — a silent zero-evidence run would mislead the operator.
  51:     """
  52:     resolved: list[dict] = []
  53:     for document_id in document_ids:
  54:         record = get_upload_record(document_id)
  55:         if record is None:
  56:             raise HTTPException(
  57:                 status_code=400,
  58:                 detail=f"uploaded document {document_id!r} not found",
  59:             )
  60:         chunks = chunk_text(record.content)
  61:         if not chunks:
  62:             raise HTTPException(
  63:                 status_code=400,
  64:                 detail=(
  65:                     f"uploaded document {document_id!r} ({record.filename}) "
  66:                     "has no extractable text — pdf/docx parsing is not yet "
  67:                     "available; upload a .md or .txt document to ground a run."
  68:                 ),
  69:             )
  70:         resolved.append(
  71:             {
  72:                 "document_id": document_id,
  73:                 "classification": record.classification,
  74:                 "filename": record.filename,
  75:                 "chunks": chunks,
  76:             }
  77:         )
  78:     return resolved
  79: 
  80: 
  81: @router.post("", response_model=RunStatusResponse, status_code=202)
  82: def create_run(payload: RunRequest) -> RunStatusResponse:
  83:     # I-rdy-010: resolve uploads BEFORE insert_run/enqueue so a bad
  84:     # document_id fails loud here instead of orphaning a queued run.
  85:     uploaded_documents = _resolve_uploaded_documents(payload.document_ids)
  86: 
  87:     run_id = uuid.uuid4().hex
  88:     try:
  89:         # I-rdy-013: atomic 1-concurrent-session gate. Returns the blocking
  90:         # active run when rejected, None when this run was inserted.
  91:         active = run_store.insert_run_if_idle(
  92:             run_id, payload.template, payload.question
  93:         )
  94:     except sqlite3.IntegrityError as exc:
  95:         # uuid4 collision is theoretically impossible but defensive
  96:         raise HTTPException(status_code=409, detail=f"run {run_id!r} already exists") from exc
  97:     except RuntimeError as exc:
  98:         # init_db permission-denied or similar
  99:         raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail=str(exc)) from exc
 100: 
 101:     if active is not None:
 102:         # I-rdy-013: 1-concurrent-session constraint — a research run is
 103:         # already queued or in progress. Reject cleanly; the rejected run is
 104:         # never enqueued (insert_run_if_idle rolled back — no row to clean
 105:         # up). The structured `detail` lets the frontend render a specific
 106:         # UX with a link to the active run.
 107:         raise HTTPException(
 108:             status_code=409,
 109:             detail={
 110:                 "code": "concurrent_run_active",
 111:                 "active_run_id": active.run_id,
 112:                 "active_status": active.lifecycle_status,
 113:                 "message": (
 114:                     "POLARIS runs one research session at a time. "
 115:                     f"Run {active.run_id[:8]} is currently {active.lifecycle_status}. "
 116:                     "Wait for it to finish before starting a new run."
 117:                 ),
 118:             },
 119:         )
 120: 
 121:     # The actor message carries the resolved upload content (the worker is
 122:     # a separate process — it cannot read the API process's upload table).
 123:     actor_payload = payload.model_dump()
 124:     actor_payload["uploaded_documents"] = uploaded_documents
 125:     try:
 126:         enqueue_research_run.send(run_id, actor_payload)
 127:     except Exception as exc:
 128:         # I-rdy-013 (Codex diff P1-001): the queued row is already committed.
 129:         # If enqueue fails it would never run yet would permanently hold the
 130:         # single-session slot. Mark it failed (terminal → frees the slot),
 131:         # then surface 503.
 132:         run_store.mark_failed(run_id, f"enqueue failed: {exc}")
 133:         raise HTTPException(
 134:             status_code=503,
 135:             detail=f"failed to enqueue run {run_id!r}: {exc}",
 136:         ) from exc
 137: 
 138:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 139:     if record is None:  # pragma: no cover — insert just succeeded
 140:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after insert")
 141:     return record
 142: 
 143: 
 144: @router.get("", response_model=list[RunStatusResponse])
 145: def list_runs(status: str = "completed", limit: int = 20) -> list[RunStatusResponse]:
 146:     """List completed runs newest-first (I-cd-705 / #705).
 147: 
 148:     Feeds the compare picker (#543), follow-up picker (#542), and the home
 149:     recent-runs strip. Only `status=completed` is supported today; aborted
 150:     runs are excluded by run_store.list_completed_runs (not
 151:     EvidenceContract-usable). `limit` is clamped to [1, 100].
 152:     """
 153:     if status != "completed":
 154:         raise HTTPException(
 155:             status_code=400,
 156:             detail="only status=completed is supported",
 157:         )
 158:     limit = max(1, min(limit, 100))
 159:     return run_store.list_completed_runs(limit=limit)
 160:

 162: @router.get("/{run_id}", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
 163: def get_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
 164:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 165:     if record is None:
 166:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
 167:     return record
 168: 
 169: 
 170: @router.post("/{run_id}/cancel", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
 171: def cancel_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
 172:     """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011 / #507).
 173: 
 174:     - Unknown run → 404.
 175:     - Already terminal (completed / failed / cancelled) → idempotent no-op,
 176:       returns the current record (200).
 177:     - queued → cancelled instantly; in_progress → cancel requested, the
 178:       worker aborts cooperatively at the next pipeline stage boundary.
 179:     """
 180:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 181:     if record is None:
 182:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
 183:     if record.lifecycle_status in run_store.TERMINAL_STATUSES:
 184:         return record  # idempotent — nothing to cancel
 185: 
 186:     run_store.request_cancel(run_id)
 187: 
 188:     updated = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 189:     if updated is None:  # pragma: no cover — the row existed a line ago

 106: def _build_tier_signals(
 107:     source: dict[str, Any],
 108: ) -> ClassificationSignals:
 109:     return ClassificationSignals(
 110:         url=source.get("url", ""),
 111:         title=source.get("title", ""),
 112:         publisher=source.get("publisher", ""),
 113:         fetched_content_length=source.get("content_length", 0),
 114:         openalex_publication_type=source.get("openalex_pub_type", ""),
 115:         openalex_source_type=source.get("openalex_source_type", ""),
 116:         openalex_is_peer_reviewed=source.get("is_peer_reviewed", False),
 117:         source_type_hint=source.get("source_type_hint", ""),
 118:     )

 121: def run_honest_pipeline(
 122:     *,
 123:     research_question: str,
 124:     domain: str,
 125:     run_id: str,
 126:     run_dir: Path | str,
 127:     retrieved_sources: list[dict[str, Any]],
 128:     evidence: list[dict[str, Any]],
 129:     draft_text: str,
 130:     approval_note: str = "",
 131:     auto_approve_if_within_bounds: bool = True,
 132: ) -> PipelineResult:
 133:     """Run the honest-rebuild pipeline end-to-end in offline mode.
 134: 
 135:     Args:
 136:         research_question: User query (verbatim).
 137:         domain: clinical / policy / tech / due_diligence.
 138:         run_id: Stable identifier.
 139:         run_dir: Directory for artifacts.
 140:         retrieved_sources: List of dicts with fields used by
 141:             tier_classifier (url / title / publisher / content_length /
 142:             openalex_pub_type / openalex_source_type / etc.) plus 'domain'.
 143:         evidence: List of evidence rows. Each dict has:
 144:             evidence_id, source_url, statement, direct_quote, tier.
 145:             (tier is populated by the tier classifier step below.)
 146:         draft_text: Prose draft with [#ev:id:start-end] provenance tokens.
 147:         approval_note: Explanation if material deviation from protocol.
 148:         auto_approve_if_within_bounds: If True and no material
 149:             deviation, approve automatically.
 150:     """
 151:     run_dir_path = Path(run_dir)
 152:     run_dir_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 153: 
 154:     # ── Phase 2b: scope gate ────────────────────────────────────────────
 155:     scope_result = run_scope_gate(
 156:         research_question=research_question,
 157:         run_dir=run_dir_path,
 158:         run_id=run_id,
 159:         domain=domain,
 160:     )
 161:     protocol_dict = scope_result.protocol.to_json_dict()
 162: 
 163:     # ── Phase 2a: tier classification of retrieved sources ─────────────
 164:     classified_sources: list[CorpusSource] = []
 165:     for src in retrieved_sources:
 166:         signals = _build_tier_signals(src)
 167:         res = classify_source_tier(signals)
 168:         classified_sources.append(CorpusSource(
 169:             url=src.get("url", ""),
 170:             title=src.get("title", ""),
 171:             domain=src.get("domain", ""),
 172:             tier=res.tier.value,
 173:             tier_confidence=res.confidence,
 174:             tier_rule=res.matched_rules[0] if res.matched_rules else "",
 175:             tier_reasons=list(res.reasons),
 176:         ))
 177: 
 178:     # Attach tier to each evidence row whose source_url matches
 179:     url_to_tier = {c.url: c.tier for c in classified_sources}
 180:     for ev in evidence:
 181:         url = ev.get("source_url", "")
 182:         if url in url_to_tier:
 183:             ev["tier"] = url_to_tier[url]
 184: 
 185:     # ── Phase 2g: corpus approval gate ──────────────────────────────────
 186:     report = compute_tier_distribution(classified_sources, protocol_dict)
 187:     approved = False
 188:     if auto_approve_if_within_bounds and not report.has_material_deviation:
 189:         approved = True
 190:     else:
 191:         ok, _ = check_auto_approve_allowed(report, approval_note)
 192:         approved = ok
 193: 
 194:     decision = CorpusApprovalDecision(
 195:         run_id=run_id,
 196:         decision_at_unix=time.time(),
 197:         decision_at_iso=time.strftime(
 198:             "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()
 199:         ),
 200:         approved=approved,
 201:         user_note=approval_note,
 202:         approved_source_urls=[s.url for s in classified_sources] if approved else [],
 203:         rejected_source_urls=[] if approved else [s.url for s in classified_sources],
 204:         report=report,
 205:         protocol_sha256=scope_result.protocol_sha256,
 206:     )
 207:     corpus_approval_path = save_approval_decision(decision, run_dir_path)
 208: 
 209:     # ── Phase 3: contradiction detection ───────────────────────────────
 210:     num_claims = extract_numeric_claims(evidence)
 211:     contradictions = detect_contradictions(num_claims)
 212:     contradictions_path = run_dir_path / "contradictions.json"
 213:     contradictions_path.write_text(
 214:         json.dumps(
 215:             [asdict(c) for c in contradictions],
 216:             indent=2, sort_keys=True, default=str,
 217:         ) + "\n",
 218:         encoding="utf-8",
 219:     )
 220: 
 221:     # ── Phase 4: strict verification of draft + resolution ─────────────
 222:     evidence_pool = {ev["evidence_id"]: ev for ev in evidence}
 223:     strict = strict_verify(draft_text, evidence_pool)
 224:     rendered_text, biblio = resolve_provenance_to_citations(
 225:         strict.kept_sentences, evidence_pool,
 226:     )
 227: 
 228:     report_path = run_dir_path / "report.md"
 229:     biblio_path = run_dir_path / "bibliography.json"
 230: 
 231:     # Augment rendered text with a methods section that includes the
 232:     # PRISMA-trAIce disclosures Phase 5 looks for.
 233:     from src.polaris_graph.llm.openrouter_client import (
 234:         PG_EVALUATOR_MODEL,
 235:         PG_GENERATOR_MODEL,
 236:     )
 237:     retrieval_date = time.strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
 238:     methods_section = (
 239:         "\n\n## Methods\n"
 240:         f"This research follows a pre-registered protocol.json artifact.\n"

  58: def _derive_slug(template_id: str, question: str) -> str:
  59:     """Deterministic URL-safe slug for pipeline-A run_dir nesting.
  60: 
  61:     Pipeline-A reads q['slug']; this produces a stable, human-readable
  62:     identifier per (template, question) pair. UUID provides uniqueness
  63:     via the artifact_dir parent — slug itself doesn't need to be unique.
  64:     """
  65:     base = f"{template_id}_{question[:60]}"
  66:     cleaned = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9_]+", "_", base.lower()).strip("_")
  67:     return cleaned[:120] or "untitled"

  70: @dramatiq.actor(max_retries=ENQUEUE_MAX_RETRIES, time_limit=30 * 60 * 1000)
  71: def enqueue_research_run(run_id: str, request_payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
  72:     """Execute a research run via pipeline-A. Idempotent on run_id.
  73: 
  74:     Stub-mode path: when run_store has no row for run_id (tests use
  75:     .fn() directly without insert_run), returns deterministic noop
  76:     without DB writes — preserves I-phase0-005 stub-mode semantics.
  77: 
  78:     Production path: marks in_progress, builds q-dict with v6 fields,

  81:     mark_completed / mark_aborted / mark_failed per pipeline_status.

  83:     # Stub-mode preservation
  84:     if run_store.get_run(run_id) is None:
  85:         return {"run_id": run_id, "status": "completed", "echo": request_payload}

  87:     # I-rdy-011 (#507): honor a cancel requested before pipeline start.

  90:     # duplicate delivery of an already-terminal run (Codex diff-iter-1 P1: a
  91:     # retry must NOT rewrite a 'failed'/'completed' row to 'cancelled'). The
  92:     # CAS itself still guards against resurrecting a just-cancelled row.
  93:     if run_store.is_cancel_requested(run_id):
  94:         run_store.mark_cancelled(run_id)
  95:         logger.info("[actor] run_id=%s cancelled before pipeline start", run_id)
  96:         return {"run_id": run_id, "status": "cancelled"}
  97:     run_store.mark_in_progress(run_id)
  98:     # A cancel may have landed in the window above; the CAS means

 100:     if run_store.is_cancel_requested(run_id):
 101:         run_store.mark_cancelled(run_id)

 succeeded in 1888ms:
   1: """Intake orchestrator — wires the front half of the research pipeline end-to-end.
   2: 
   3: Per slice 001 architecture proposal §"Implementation order PR 6". The
   4: function process_intake() is the single entry point that transforms a
   5: raw user-typed string into a ScopeDecision ready for the UI.
   6: 
   7: Pipeline (deterministic order):
   8: 
   9:     raw_question (str)
  10:         ↓
  11:     question_normalizer.normalize()
  12:         ↓ NormalizedQuestion (NFC + whitespace + control-stripped + length-bounded)
  13:         ↓
  14:     clinical_classifier.classify()
  15:         ↓ RegexClassifyResult (refused | clinical_* | out_of_scope | uncertain)
  16:         ↓
  17:     [if refused] → assemble_scope_decision(refused=True)
  18:     [if out_of_scope] → assemble_scope_decision(scope_class=out_of_scope, ambiguity=None)
  19:     [if clinical_*]:
  20:         ambiguity_detector_clinical.detect_ambiguity()
  21:             ↓ AmbiguityAxes
  22:             ↓
  23:         assemble_scope_decision(scope_class=..., ambiguity=...)
  24:         ↓
  25:     ScopeDecision
  26: 
  27: Latency is measured wall-clock (intake → decision) and threaded into
  28: ScopeDecision.latency_ms.
  29: 
  30: Errors during normalization (QuestionTooShort, QuestionTooLong) are
  31: surfaced as IntakeError with a structured reason so the UI can show
  32: helpful guidance.
  33: """
  34: 
  35: from __future__ import annotations
  36: 
  37: import time
  38: from dataclasses import dataclass
  39: from typing import Callable
  40: 
  41: from polaris_graph.intake.question_normalizer import (
  42:     QuestionTooLong,
  43:     QuestionTooShort,
  44:     normalize,
  45: )
  46: from polaris_graph.scope.ambiguity_detector_clinical import detect_ambiguity
  47: from polaris_graph.scope.clinical_classifier import classify
  48: from polaris_graph.scope.scope_decision import (
  49:     AmbiguityAxis,
  50:     AmbiguityAxes,
  51:     ScopeDecision,
  52:     assemble_scope_decision,
  53: )
  54: 
  55: 
  56: @dataclass(frozen=True)
  57: class IntakeError:
  58:     """Surfaced when the question cannot be processed (e.g., too short/long).
  59: 
  60:     Not the same as out_of_scope or refused — those are valid ScopeDecisions.
  61:     IntakeError indicates the question never reached the classifier.
  62:     """
  63: 
  64:     code: str  # 'too_short' | 'too_long' | 'invalid_input'
  65:     message: str  # human-readable for UI
  66:     raw: str  # original user input
  67: 
  68: 
  69: def _empty_axes() -> AmbiguityAxes:
  70:     """Default AmbiguityAxes used for refused / out_of_scope paths
  71:     (downstream UI doesn't render the modal in those cases)."""
  72:     blank = AmbiguityAxis(
  73:         axis="population",
  74:         plausible_interpretations=["n/a"],
  75:         needs_clarification=False,
  76:     )
  77:     return AmbiguityAxes(
  78:         population=AmbiguityAxis(
  79:             axis="population", plausible_interpretations=["n/a"], needs_clarification=False
  80:         ),
  81:         intervention=AmbiguityAxis(
  82:             axis="intervention", plausible_interpretations=["n/a"], needs_clarification=False
  83:         ),
  84:         outcome=AmbiguityAxis(
  85:             axis="outcome", plausible_interpretations=["n/a"], needs_clarification=False
  86:         ),
  87:         is_ambiguous=False,
  88:     )
  89: 
  90: 
  91: def process_intake(
  92:     raw_question: str,
  93:     *,
  94:     completion_fn: Callable[[str], str] | None = None,
  95: ) -> ScopeDecision | IntakeError:
  96:     """Orchestrate the front-half ambiguity-detection pipeline.
  97: 
  98:     Args:
  99:         raw_question: user-typed input, any string. Will be normalized.
 100:         completion_fn: optional dependency-injectable LLM call for the
 101:                        classifier's LLM fallback layer. Tests pass mocks;
 102:                        production uses the default OpenRouter client.
 103: 
 104:     Returns:
 105:         ScopeDecision on success (any status: in_scope / out_of_scope /
 106:         ambiguous_needs_clarification / refused).
 107:         IntakeError if the question is malformed (too short, too long,
 108:         or non-string).
 109:     """
 110:     t_start = time.perf_counter()
 111: 
 112:     # Step 1: normalize
 113:     try:
 114:         normalized = normalize(raw_question)
 115:     except QuestionTooShort:
 116:         return IntakeError(
 117:             code="too_short",
 118:             message="Please enter a longer question (at least 3 characters).",
 119:             raw=raw_question if isinstance(raw_question, str) else "",
 120:         )
 121:     except QuestionTooLong:
 122:         return IntakeError(
 123:             code="too_long",
 124:             message="Question is too long. Please shorten to at most 1000 characters.",
 125:             raw=raw_question if isinstance(raw_question, str) else "",
 126:         )
 127:     except TypeError:
 128:         return IntakeError(
 129:             code="invalid_input",
 130:             message="Question must be a text string.",
 131:             raw=str(raw_question)[:200] if raw_question is not None else "",
 132:         )
 133: 
 134:     # Step 2: classify (regex layer + LLM fallback if uncertain)
 135:     classifier_result = classify(
 136:         normalized.normalized,
 137:         completion_fn=completion_fn,
 138:     )
 139: 
 140:     # Step 3: refused short-circuit
 141:     if classifier_result.refused:
 142:         latency = int((time.perf_counter() - t_start) * 1000)
 143:         return assemble_scope_decision(
 144:             scope_class=None,
 145:             ambiguity=None,
 146:             refused=True,
 147:             refusal_reason="instruction_override_attempt",
 148:             latency_ms=latency,
 149:         )
 150: 
 151:     # Step 4: out_of_scope path (no ambiguity detection needed)
 152:     if classifier_result.scope_class.value == "out_of_scope":
 153:         latency = int((time.perf_counter() - t_start) * 1000)
 154:         return assemble_scope_decision(
 155:             scope_class=classifier_result.scope_class,
 156:             ambiguity=None,
 157:             latency_ms=latency,
 158:         )
 159: 
 160:     # Step 5: uncertain after both regex + LLM — surface as out_of_scope
 161:     # rather than guessing. UI shows the standard out-of-scope message.
 162:     if classifier_result.scope_class.value == "uncertain":
 163:         latency = int((time.perf_counter() - t_start) * 1000)
 164:         # Treat uncertain as out_of_scope for slice 1 (graceful fallback —
 165:         # don't pretend to handle questions we couldn't classify)
 166:         from polaris_graph.scope.scope_decision import ScopeClass
 167: 
 168:         oos_class = ScopeClass(
 169:             value="out_of_scope",
 170:             confidence=classifier_result.scope_class.confidence,
 171:             provenance=classifier_result.scope_class.provenance,
 172:             matched_pattern=None,
 173:         )
 174:         return assemble_scope_decision(
 175:             scope_class=oos_class,
 176:             ambiguity=None,
 177:             latency_ms=latency,
 178:         )
 179: 
 180:     # Step 6: clinical_* — run ambiguity detection
 181:     axes = detect_ambiguity(normalized.normalized)
 182:     latency = int((time.perf_counter() - t_start) * 1000)
 183:     return assemble_scope_decision(
 184:         scope_class=classifier_result.scope_class,
 185:         ambiguity=axes,
 186:         latency_ms=latency,
 187:     )

 succeeded in 1933ms:
   1: """Scope decision schema + assembly.
   2: 
   3: Per slice 001 architecture proposal §"Data shapes". Defines the canonical
   4: Pydantic types that flow through the front half of the research pipeline:
   5: 
   6:     NormalizedQuestion (intake)
   7:         ↓
   8:     ScopeClass + AmbiguityAxes (classifier + detector — later PRs)
   9:         ↓
  10:     ScopeDecision (assembled here)
  11: 
  12: The schemas exactly match the golden test bundle's expected_scope_decision
  13: shape (polaris-controls/golden/slice_001/test_*.json) so CI can deep-equal.
  14: 
  15: Pure-types module: no I/O, no network, no LLM calls. Validation only.
  16: """
  17: 
  18: from __future__ import annotations
  19: 
  20: import uuid
  21: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  22: from typing import Literal
  23: 
  24: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, field_validator
  25: 
  26: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  27: # Type literals
  28: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  29: 
  30: PicoAxis = Literal["population", "intervention", "outcome"]
  31: """The three PICO axes used by slice 001's ambiguity detector. Comparator
  32: is intentionally excluded — it's a slice-2+ retrieval concern."""
  33: 
  34: ScopeClassValue = Literal[
  35:     "clinical_efficacy",
  36:     "clinical_safety",
  37:     "clinical_diagnosis",
  38:     "clinical_prognosis",
  39:     "out_of_scope",
  40:     "uncertain",
  41: ]
  42: """Coarse-grained classification of a question's scope. Slice 001 emits
  43: one of these per question; downstream slices may refine or extend."""
  44: 
  45: ScopeStatus = Literal[
  46:     "in_scope",
  47:     "out_of_scope",
  48:     "ambiguous_needs_clarification",
  49:     "refused",
  50: ]
  51: """Final disposition surfaced to the UI. Discriminated-union shape forces
  52: explicit handling of all four cases (rather than booleans + flags). The
  53: golden test suite asserts exactly one of these as expected_scope_decision.status."""
  54: 
  55: 
  56: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  57: # Component schemas
  58: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  59: 
  60: class ScopeClass(BaseModel):
  61:     """Output of the classifier layer."""
  62: 
  63:     value: ScopeClassValue = Field(description="Coarse-grained scope class")
  64:     confidence: float = Field(
  65:         description="Classifier confidence in [0.0, 1.0]; regex hit = 1.0",
  66:         ge=0.0, le=1.0,
  67:     )
  68:     provenance: Literal["regex", "llm_fallback"] = Field(
  69:         description="Which classifier layer produced this verdict"
  70:     )
  71:     matched_pattern: str | None = Field(
  72:         default=None,
  73:         description="For regex hits, the pattern name. Null for LLM fallback.",
  74:     )
  75: 
  76: 
  77: class AmbiguityAxis(BaseModel):
  78:     """One PICO axis's ambiguity assessment."""
  79: 
  80:     axis: PicoAxis = Field(description="Which PICO axis")
  81:     plausible_interpretations: list[str] = Field(
  82:         description="Distinct interpretations the question could plausibly mean"
  83:     )
  84:     needs_clarification: bool = Field(
  85:         description="True iff len(plausible_interpretations) > 1"
  86:     )
  87: 
  88:     @field_validator("plausible_interpretations")
  89:     @classmethod
  90:     def _validate_interpretations_nonempty(cls, v: list[str]) -> list[str]:
  91:         # Empty list is invalid — even a clear axis has 1 interpretation
  92:         if not v:
  93:             raise ValueError("plausible_interpretations must have at least 1 entry")
  94:         # Cap at 5 to keep the modal UI reasonable per architecture proposal
  95:         if len(v) > 5:
  96:             raise ValueError(
  97:                 f"plausible_interpretations capped at 5; got {len(v)}"
  98:             )
  99:         return v
 100: 
 101: 
 102: class AmbiguityAxes(BaseModel):
 103:     """Per-PICO ambiguity. Slice 001 uses three axes (P/I/O); Comparator
 104:     is a slice-2+ retrieval concern."""
 105: 
 106:     population: AmbiguityAxis
 107:     intervention: AmbiguityAxis
 108:     outcome: AmbiguityAxis
 109:     is_ambiguous: bool = Field(
 110:         description="True iff any axis has needs_clarification=True"
 111:     )
 112: 
 113:     @field_validator("population", "intervention", "outcome")
 114:     @classmethod
 115:     def _validate_axis_matches_field(cls, v: AmbiguityAxis, info) -> AmbiguityAxis:
 116:         if v.axis != info.field_name:
 117:             raise ValueError(
 118:                 f"AmbiguityAxes.{info.field_name} must have axis='{info.field_name}', got '{v.axis}'"
 119:             )
 120:         return v
 121: 
 122: 
 123: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 124: # Top-level decision
 125: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 126: 
 127: class ScopeDecision(BaseModel):
 128:     """Final assembled output of slice 001's front-half pipeline.
 129: 
 130:     Shape matches polaris-controls/golden/slice_001/test_*.json
 131:     expected_scope_decision exactly so CI can deep-equal compare.
 132:     """
 133: 
 134:     status: ScopeStatus = Field(description="Final disposition for UI")
 135:     scope_class: ScopeClassValue | None = Field(
 136:         default=None,
 137:         description="None when status == 'out_of_scope' or 'refused'",
 138:     )
 139:     ambiguity_axes: list[AmbiguityAxis] = Field(
 140:         default_factory=list,
 141:         description="Ordered P/I/O axes; empty when out_of_scope/refused",
 142:     )
 143:     clarifications_needed: list[str] = Field(
 144:         default_factory=list,
 145:         description="Human-readable strings shown in the AmbiguityModal",
 146:     )
 147:     provenance: dict[str, str] = Field(
 148:         default_factory=dict,
 149:         description="Layer-trace dict: classifier_layer, ambiguity_detector_layer, etc.",
 150:     )
 151:     decision_id: str = Field(
 152:         default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()),
 153:         description="Unique ID for this decision; used in logging/audit-bundle",
 154:     )
 155:     decided_at_utc: datetime = Field(
 156:         default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(timezone.utc),
 157:         description="UTC timestamp at decision time",
 158:     )
 159:     latency_ms: int = Field(
 160:         default=0,
 161:         ge=0,
 162:         description="Wall-clock time intake → decision in milliseconds",
 163:     )
 164: 
 165: 
 166: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 167: # Assembly helper
 168: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 169: 
 170: def assemble_scope_decision(
 171:     scope_class: ScopeClass | None,
 172:     ambiguity: AmbiguityAxes | None,
 173:     *,
 174:     refused: bool = False,
 175:     refusal_reason: str | None = None,
 176:     latency_ms: int = 0,
 177: ) -> ScopeDecision:
 178:     """Combine classifier output + ambiguity output into final decision.
 179: 
 180:     Logic (per architecture proposal):
 181:         - If refused=True → status='refused', no class, no axes
 182:         - If scope_class.value == 'out_of_scope' → status='out_of_scope'
 183:         - Elif ambiguity.is_ambiguous → status='ambiguous_needs_clarification'
 184:         - Else → status='in_scope'
 185:     """
 186:     if refused:
 187:         return ScopeDecision(
 188:             status="refused",
 189:             scope_class=None,
 190:             ambiguity_axes=[],
 191:             clarifications_needed=[],
 192:             provenance={"refusal_reason": refusal_reason or "instruction_override_attempt"},
 193:             latency_ms=latency_ms,
 194:         )
 195: 
 196:     if scope_class is None:
 197:         # Defensive — caller should always supply scope_class except in refused path
 198:         raise ValueError("scope_class is required when not refused")
 199: 
 200:     if scope_class.value == "out_of_scope":
 201:         return ScopeDecision(
 202:             status="out_of_scope",
 203:             scope_class=None,  # per architecture proposal: None when out_of_scope/refused
 204:             ambiguity_axes=[],
 205:             clarifications_needed=[],
 206:             provenance={
 207:                 "classifier_layer": scope_class.provenance,
 208:                 "out_of_scope_reason": "no_clinical_pico_pattern_matched",
 209:             },
 210:             latency_ms=latency_ms,
 211:         )
 212: 
 213:     if ambiguity is None:
 214:         raise ValueError("ambiguity is required when scope_class is in-scope")
 215: 
 216:     axes = [ambiguity.population, ambiguity.intervention, ambiguity.outcome]
 217:     clarifications = [
 218:         f"Which {ax.axis}: {', '.join(ax.plausible_interpretations)}?"
 219:         for ax in axes if ax.needs_clarification
 220:     ]
 221: 
 222:     status: ScopeStatus = (
 223:         "ambiguous_needs_clarification"
 224:         if ambiguity.is_ambiguous
 225:         else "in_scope"
 226:     )
 227: 
 228:     return ScopeDecision(
 229:         status=status,
 230:         scope_class=scope_class.value,
 231:         ambiguity_axes=axes,
 232:         clarifications_needed=clarifications,
 233:         provenance={
 234:             "classifier_layer": scope_class.provenance,
 235:             "ambiguity_detector_layer": "pico_axes_v1",
 236:         },
 237:         latency_ms=latency_ms,
 238:     )

   1: "use client";

   3: import { useEffect, useRef } from "react";

   8: 
   9: const MAX_SAMPLE_LEN = 80;
  10: 
  11: export type DisambiguationModalProps = {
  12:   open: boolean;
  13:   clusters: DisambiguationCluster[];
  14:   onSelectCluster: (cluster_id: number) => void;
  15:   onCancel: () => void;
  16: };
  17: 
  18: function previewSnippets(snippets: string[]): string {
  19:   const joined = snippets.slice(0, 2).join(" · ");
  20:   return joined.length > MAX_SAMPLE_LEN
  21:     ? joined.slice(0, MAX_SAMPLE_LEN - 1) + "…"
  22:     : joined;
  23: }
  24: 
  25: export function DisambiguationModal({
  26:   open,
  27:   clusters,
  28:   onSelectCluster,
  29:   onCancel,
  30: }: DisambiguationModalProps) {
  31:   const is_cancelled_ref = useRef(false);
  32:   useEffect(() => {
  33:     if (open) is_cancelled_ref.current = false;
  34:   }, [open]);

 156: # BUG-B-101 fix: unified manifest.status taxonomy.
 157: #
 158: # Pre-fix, successful runs wrote manifest.json WITHOUT a "status" key
 159: # while abort runs DID include it. Documentation claimed
 160: # manifest.status was authoritative — it wasn't. See
 161: # outputs/codex_findings/deep_dive_round_1/findings.md for the full
 162: # scoping analysis.
 163: #
 164: # Post-fix, EVERY exit path writes a manifest.json with a "status"
 165: # field from this unified taxonomy. `summary["status"]` is preserved
 166: # as secondary sweep telemetry for backward compatibility with any
 167: # downstream counter that relied on the legacy labels.
 168: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 169: 
 170: UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES: frozenset[str] = frozenset({
 171:     # success
 172:     "success",
 173:     # partial — report produced but degraded signal
 174:     "partial_thin_corpus",
 175:     "partial_incomplete_corpus",
 176:     "partial_rule_check_warnings",
 177:     "partial_outline_fallback",      # BUG-M-203: planner failed, fallback used
 178:     "partial_evaluator_advisory",    # BUG-M-205: judge flagged critical axes
 179:     "partial_qwen_advisory",         # I-modref-004 (#530): legacy alias, historical manifests
 180:     # abort — pipeline refused to produce a report
 181:     "abort_scope_rejected",
 182:     "abort_no_sources",
 183:     "abort_corpus_inadequate",
 184:     "abort_corpus_approval_denied",
 185:     "abort_no_verified_sections",
 186:     "abort_evaluator_critical",      # BUG-M-205: PT08/PT11/PT12 integrity failure
 187:     # error — unhandled exception
 188:     "error_unexpected",
 189: })
 190:

 195:     "ok_incomplete_corpus": "partial_incomplete_corpus",

 211: def to_unified_status(summary_status: str) -> str:
 212:     """Map a legacy summary["status"] label to the unified
 213:     manifest.status taxonomy. Unknown labels become error_unexpected
 214:     (fail loudly for the reader; still a valid taxonomy value)."""
 215:     return _SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED.get(summary_status, "error_unexpected")

 218: def expected_str_for_abort(protocol: dict) -> str:
 219:     """Render expected tier distribution for abort-artifact text."""
 220:     parts = []
 221:     for entry in protocol.get("expected_tier_distribution", []) or []:
 222:         tier = entry.get("tier")
 223:         mn = (entry.get("min_fraction", 0) or 0) * 100
 224:         mx = (entry.get("max_fraction", 1) or 1) * 100
 225:         if tier:
 226:             parts.append(f"{tier} {mn:.0f}-{mx:.0f}%")
 227:     return ", ".join(parts) or "per scope template"

 230: def _base_manifest_envelope(
 231:     *,
 232:     run_id: str,
 233:     q: dict,
 234:     retrieval=None,
 235:     run_cost: float = 0.0,
 236: ) -> dict:
 237:     """BUG-SCHEMA-R8d fix: every manifest (success AND abort) carries
 238:     the same envelope so downstream consumers get consistent keys
 239:     regardless of exit path.
 240: 
 241:     Caller adds status-specific fields on top (adequacy, generator,
 242:     evaluator_gate, scope, error, etc.). Using this helper prevents
 243:     the envelope from drifting between exit paths.
 244:     """
 245:     env: dict = {
 246:         "run_id": run_id,
 247:         "slug": q.get("slug", ""),
 248:         "domain": q.get("domain", ""),
 249:         "question": q.get("question", ""),
 250:         "cost_usd": run_cost,
 251:         "budget_cap_usd": PG_MAX_COST_PER_RUN,
 252:     }
 253:     if retrieval is not None:
 254:         env["retrieval"] = {
 255:             "pre_filter": getattr(retrieval, "total_candidates_pre_filter", 0),
 256:             "fetched": getattr(retrieval, "candidates_fetched", 0),
 257:             "failed": getattr(retrieval, "candidates_failed_fetch", 0),
 258:             "api_calls": getattr(retrieval, "api_calls", {}),
 259:         }
 260:     return env
 261: 
 262: 
 263: def write_per_run_cost_ledger(run_dir: Path, run_id: str) -> int:
 264:     """BUG-M-206 fix (deep-dive R8): filter the global cost ledger for
 265:     entries tagged with this run_id and write a per-run copy to
 266:     <run_dir>/cost_ledger.jsonl. Returns the count of entries written.
 267: 
 268:     The global ledger stays authoritative (monotonic append-only log),
 269:     but per-run consumers don't have to grep it by run_id anymore.
 270:     """
 271:     global_path = Path(
 272:         os.environ.get("PG_COST_LEDGER_PATH", "logs/pg_cost_ledger.jsonl")
 273:     )
 274:     if not global_path.exists():
 275:         return 0
 276:     out_path = run_dir / "cost_ledger.jsonl"
 277:     n = 0
 278:     try:
 279:         with open(global_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as src, \
 280:                 open(out_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as dst:
 281:             for line in src:
 282:                 line = line.rstrip("\n")
 283:                 if not line:
 284:                     continue
 285:                 try:
 286:                     entry = json.loads(line)
 287:                 except json.JSONDecodeError:
 288:                     continue
 289:                 if entry.get("session_id") == run_id:
 290:                     dst.write(line + "\n")
 291:                     n += 1
 292:     except OSError as exc:
 293:         logging.getLogger(__name__).warning(
 294:             "per-run cost ledger write failed: %s", exc,
 295:         )
 296:     return n
 297: 
 298: 
 299: def filter_verified_sections(sections) -> list:
 300:     """Codex round 1 B-3: the single-source-of-truth predicate for
 301:     "did this section survive Phase-4 strict_verify?". A section
 302:     qualifies only if it was NOT dropped AND has non-empty verified_text.
 303:     """
 304:     return [
 305:         sr for sr in sections
 306:         if not getattr(sr, "dropped_due_to_failure", True)
 307:         and getattr(sr, "verified_text", "")
 308:     ]
